translation of BSSN_RHS.nb from Zach Etienne's SENR project, from Mathematica into Lua symmath

SHIFTADVECT = true
BIADVECT = true
CFEvolution = EvolveW
CoordSystem = SphericalPolar
InitialDataType = Minkowski
InitialLapseType = PunctureR2
InitialShiftType = Zero
${{r_{coord}}} = {r}$
${{\theta_{coord}}} = {\theta}$
${{\phi_{coord}}} = {\phi}$
$y^i = \{$ $r$ $\theta$ $\phi$ $\}$
coordinate basis $x^i = \{$ $r$, $\theta$, $\phi$ $\}$
non-coordinate basis $x^I = \{$ $\hat{r}$, $\hat{\theta}$, $\hat{\phi}$ $\}$
Using capital letters to denote sums over non-coordinate basis.
Using hats to denote individual non-coordinate basis terms.
Rescaling transform to non-coordinate basis:
${{{e}^I}_i} = {\overset{I\downarrow i\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} 1 & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & r & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & {{r}} {{sin\left(\theta\right)}} \end{matrix} \right] }}$
${{{e}_I}^i} = {\overset{I\downarrow i\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} 1 & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & \frac{1}{r} & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & \frac{1}{{{r}} {{sin\left(\theta\right)}}} \end{matrix} \right] }}$
grid metric:
${{{\hat{\gamma}}_i}_j} = {\overset{i\downarrow j\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} 1 & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & {r}^{2} & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & {{{r}^{2}}} {{{sin\left(\theta\right)}^{2}}} \end{matrix} \right] }}$
${{{\hat{\gamma}}^i}^j} = {\overset{i\downarrow j\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} 1 & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & \frac{1}{{r}^{2}} & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & \frac{1}{{{{r}^{2}}} {{{sin\left(\theta\right)}^{2}}}} \end{matrix} \right] }}$

${{{{\hat{\Gamma}}^i}_j}_k} = {{{{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{\hat{\gamma}}^i}^m}}}} {{({{{{{{\hat{\gamma}}_m}_j}_{,k}} + {{{{\hat{\gamma}}_m}_k}_{,j}}} - {{{{\hat{\gamma}}_j}_k}_{,m}}})}}}$
${{{{\hat{\Gamma}}^i}_j}_k} = {\overset{i\downarrow[{j\downarrow k\rightarrow}]}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} \left[ \begin{matrix} 0 & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & -{r} & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & -{{{r}} {{{sin\left(\theta\right)}^{2}}}} \end{matrix} \right] \\ \left[ \begin{matrix} 0 & \frac{1}{r} & 0 \\ \frac{1}{r} & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & -{{{sin\left(\theta\right)}} {{cos\left(\theta\right)}}} \end{matrix} \right] \\ \left[ \begin{matrix} 0 & 0 & \frac{1}{r} \\ 0 & 0 & \frac{cos\left(\theta\right)}{sin\left(\theta\right)} \\ \frac{1}{r} & \frac{cos\left(\theta\right)}{sin\left(\theta\right)} & 0 \end{matrix} \right] \end{matrix} \right] }}$
${{{{{\hat{\Gamma}}^i}_j}_k}_{,l}} = {\overset{i\downarrow j\rightarrow[{k\downarrow l\rightarrow}]}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} \overset{k\downarrow l\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} 0 & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & 0 \end{matrix} \right] } & \overset{k\downarrow l\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} 0 & 0 & 0 \\ -{1} & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & 0 \end{matrix} \right] } & \overset{k\downarrow l\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} 0 & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & 0 \\ -{{sin\left(\theta\right)}^{2}} & -{{{2}} {{r}} {{sin\left(\theta\right)}} {{cos\left(\theta\right)}}} & 0 \end{matrix} \right] } \\ \overset{k\downarrow l\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} 0 & 0 & 0 \\ -{\frac{1}{{r}^{2}}} & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & 0 \end{matrix} \right] } & \overset{k\downarrow l\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} -{\frac{1}{{r}^{2}}} & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & 0 \end{matrix} \right] } & \overset{k\downarrow l\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} 0 & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & -{({{1} - {{{2}} {{{sin\left(\theta\right)}^{2}}}}})} & 0 \end{matrix} \right] } \\ \overset{k\downarrow l\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} 0 & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & 0 \\ -{\frac{1}{{r}^{2}}} & 0 & 0 \end{matrix} \right] } & \overset{k\downarrow l\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} 0 & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & -{\frac{1}{{sin\left(\theta\right)}^{2}}} & 0 \end{matrix} \right] } & \overset{k\downarrow l\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} -{\frac{1}{{r}^{2}}} & 0 & 0 \\ 0 & -{\frac{1}{{sin\left(\theta\right)}^{2}}} & 0 \\ 0 & 0 & 0 \end{matrix} \right] } \end{matrix} \right] }}$
state variables:
${{{h}_I}_J} = {\overset{I\downarrow J\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} {h_{\hat{r} \hat{r}}} & {h_{\hat{r} \hat{\theta}}} & {h_{\hat{r} \hat{\phi}}} \\ {h_{\hat{r} \hat{\theta}}} & {h_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\theta}}} & {h_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\phi}}} \\ {h_{\hat{r} \hat{\phi}}} & {h_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\phi}}} & {h_{\hat{\phi} \hat{\phi}}} \end{matrix} \right] }}$
${{{{h}_I}_J}_{,k}} = {\overset{I\downarrow[{J\downarrow k\rightarrow}]}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} \overset{J\downarrow k\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} {h_{\hat{r} \hat{r}}}_{,{{r}}} & {h_{\hat{r} \hat{r}}}_{,{{\theta}}} & {h_{\hat{r} \hat{r}}}_{,{{\phi}}} \\ {h_{\hat{r} \hat{\theta}}}_{,{{r}}} & {h_{\hat{r} \hat{\theta}}}_{,{{\theta}}} & {h_{\hat{r} \hat{\theta}}}_{,{{\phi}}} \\ {h_{\hat{r} \hat{\phi}}}_{,{{r}}} & {h_{\hat{r} \hat{\phi}}}_{,{{\theta}}} & {h_{\hat{r} \hat{\phi}}}_{,{{\phi}}} \end{matrix} \right] } \\ \overset{J\downarrow k\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} {h_{\hat{r} \hat{\theta}}}_{,{{r}}} & {h_{\hat{r} \hat{\theta}}}_{,{{\theta}}} & {h_{\hat{r} \hat{\theta}}}_{,{{\phi}}} \\ {h_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\theta}}}_{,{{r}}} & {h_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\theta}}}_{,{{\theta}}} & {h_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\theta}}}_{,{{\phi}}} \\ {h_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\phi}}}_{,{{r}}} & {h_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\phi}}}_{,{{\theta}}} & {h_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\phi}}}_{,{{\phi}}} \end{matrix} \right] } \\ \overset{J\downarrow k\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} {h_{\hat{r} \hat{\phi}}}_{,{{r}}} & {h_{\hat{r} \hat{\phi}}}_{,{{\theta}}} & {h_{\hat{r} \hat{\phi}}}_{,{{\phi}}} \\ {h_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\phi}}}_{,{{r}}} & {h_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\phi}}}_{,{{\theta}}} & {h_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\phi}}}_{,{{\phi}}} \\ {h_{\hat{\phi} \hat{\phi}}}_{,{{r}}} & {h_{\hat{\phi} \hat{\phi}}}_{,{{\theta}}} & {h_{\hat{\phi} \hat{\phi}}}_{,{{\phi}}} \end{matrix} \right] } \end{matrix} \right] }}$
${{{a}_I}_J} = {\overset{I\downarrow J\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} {a_{\hat{r} \hat{r}}} & {a_{\hat{r} \hat{\theta}}} & {a_{\hat{r} \hat{\phi}}} \\ {a_{\hat{r} \hat{\theta}}} & {a_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\theta}}} & {a_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\phi}}} \\ {a_{\hat{r} \hat{\phi}}} & {a_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\phi}}} & {a_{\hat{\phi} \hat{\phi}}} \end{matrix} \right] }}$

${{{\epsilon}_i}_j} = {{{{{{{h}_I}_J}} {{{{e}^I}_i}}}} {{{{e}^J}_j}}}$
${{{\epsilon}_i}_j} = {\overset{i\downarrow j\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} {h_{\hat{r} \hat{r}}} & {{{h_{\hat{r} \hat{\theta}}}}} \cdot {{r}} & {{{h_{\hat{r} \hat{\phi}}}}} \cdot {{r}} {{sin\left(\theta\right)}} \\ {{{h_{\hat{r} \hat{\theta}}}}} \cdot {{r}} & {{{h_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\theta}}}}} \cdot {{{r}^{2}}} & {{{h_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\phi}}}}} \cdot {{{r}^{2}}} {{sin\left(\theta\right)}} \\ {{{h_{\hat{r} \hat{\phi}}}}} \cdot {{r}} {{sin\left(\theta\right)}} & {{{h_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\phi}}}}} \cdot {{{r}^{2}}} {{sin\left(\theta\right)}} & {{{h_{\hat{\phi} \hat{\phi}}}}} \cdot {{{r}^{2}}} {{{sin\left(\theta\right)}^{2}}} \end{matrix} \right] }}$

${{{\bar{\gamma}}_i}_j} = {{{{\hat{\gamma}}_i}_j} + {{{\epsilon}_i}_j}}$
${{{\bar{\gamma}}_i}_j} = {\overset{i\downarrow j\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} {1} + {{h_{\hat{r} \hat{r}}}} & {{{h_{\hat{r} \hat{\theta}}}}} \cdot {{r}} & {{{h_{\hat{r} \hat{\phi}}}}} \cdot {{r}} {{sin\left(\theta\right)}} \\ {{{h_{\hat{r} \hat{\theta}}}}} \cdot {{r}} & {{{r}^{2}}} {{({{1} + {{h_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\theta}}}}})}} & {{{h_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\phi}}}}} \cdot {{{r}^{2}}} {{sin\left(\theta\right)}} \\ {{{h_{\hat{r} \hat{\phi}}}}} \cdot {{r}} {{sin\left(\theta\right)}} & {{{h_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\phi}}}}} \cdot {{{r}^{2}}} {{sin\left(\theta\right)}} & {{{r}^{2}}} {{{sin\left(\theta\right)}^{2}}} {{({{1} + {{h_{\hat{\phi} \hat{\phi}}}}})}} \end{matrix} \right] }}$

${{{\bar{A}}_i}_j} = {{{{{{{a}_I}_J}} {{{{e}^I}_i}}}} {{{{e}^J}_j}}}$
${{{\bar{A}}_i}_j} = {\overset{i\downarrow j\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} {a_{\hat{r} \hat{r}}} & {{{a_{\hat{r} \hat{\theta}}}}} \cdot {{r}} & {{{a_{\hat{r} \hat{\phi}}}}} \cdot {{r}} {{sin\left(\theta\right)}} \\ {{{a_{\hat{r} \hat{\theta}}}}} \cdot {{r}} & {{{a_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\theta}}}}} \cdot {{{r}^{2}}} & {{{a_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\phi}}}}} \cdot {{{r}^{2}}} {{sin\left(\theta\right)}} \\ {{{a_{\hat{r} \hat{\phi}}}}} \cdot {{r}} {{sin\left(\theta\right)}} & {{{a_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\phi}}}}} \cdot {{{r}^{2}}} {{sin\left(\theta\right)}} & {{{a_{\hat{\phi} \hat{\phi}}}}} \cdot {{{r}^{2}}} {{{sin\left(\theta\right)}^{2}}} \end{matrix} \right] }}$
${{{{\epsilon}_i}_j}_{,k}} = {\overset{i\downarrow[{j\downarrow k\rightarrow}]}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} \overset{j\downarrow k\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} {h_{\hat{r} \hat{r}}}_{,{{r}}} & {h_{\hat{r} \hat{r}}}_{,{{\theta}}} & {h_{\hat{r} \hat{r}}}_{,{{\phi}}} \\ {{h_{\hat{r} \hat{\theta}}}} + {{{r}} {{{h_{\hat{r} \hat{\theta}}}_{,{{r}}}}}} & {{{h_{\hat{r} \hat{\theta}}}_{,{{\theta}}}}} {{r}} & {{{h_{\hat{r} \hat{\theta}}}_{,{{\phi}}}}} {{r}} \\ {{sin\left(\theta\right)}} {{({{{h_{\hat{r} \hat{\phi}}}} + {{{r}} {{{h_{\hat{r} \hat{\phi}}}_{,{{r}}}}}}})}} & {{r}} {{({{{{cos\left(\theta\right)}} {{{h_{\hat{r} \hat{\phi}}}}}} + {{{sin\left(\theta\right)}} {{{h_{\hat{r} \hat{\phi}}}_{,{{\theta}}}}}}})}} & {{{h_{\hat{r} \hat{\phi}}}_{,{{\phi}}}}} {{r}} {{sin\left(\theta\right)}} \end{matrix} \right] } \\ \overset{j\downarrow k\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} {{h_{\hat{r} \hat{\theta}}}} + {{{r}} {{{h_{\hat{r} \hat{\theta}}}_{,{{r}}}}}} & {{{h_{\hat{r} \hat{\theta}}}_{,{{\theta}}}}} {{r}} & {{{h_{\hat{r} \hat{\theta}}}_{,{{\phi}}}}} {{r}} \\ {{r}} {{({{{{r}} {{{h_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\theta}}}_{,{{r}}}}}} + {{{2}} {{{h_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\theta}}}}}}})}} & {{{h_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\theta}}}_{,{{\theta}}}}} {{{r}^{2}}} & {{{h_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\theta}}}_{,{{\phi}}}}} {{{r}^{2}}} \\ {{r}} {{sin\left(\theta\right)}} {{({{{{r}} {{{h_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\phi}}}_{,{{r}}}}}} + {{{2}} {{{h_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\phi}}}}}}})}} & {{{r}^{2}}} {{({{{{cos\left(\theta\right)}} {{{h_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\phi}}}}}} + {{{sin\left(\theta\right)}} {{{h_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\phi}}}_{,{{\theta}}}}}}})}} & {{{h_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\phi}}}_{,{{\phi}}}}} {{{r}^{2}}} {{sin\left(\theta\right)}} \end{matrix} \right] } \\ \overset{j\downarrow k\rightarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} {{sin\left(\theta\right)}} {{({{{h_{\hat{r} \hat{\phi}}}} + {{{r}} {{{h_{\hat{r} \hat{\phi}}}_{,{{r}}}}}}})}} & {{r}} {{({{{{cos\left(\theta\right)}} {{{h_{\hat{r} \hat{\phi}}}}}} + {{{sin\left(\theta\right)}} {{{h_{\hat{r} \hat{\phi}}}_{,{{\theta}}}}}}})}} & {{{h_{\hat{r} \hat{\phi}}}_{,{{\phi}}}}} {{r}} {{sin\left(\theta\right)}} \\ {{r}} {{sin\left(\theta\right)}} {{({{{{r}} {{{h_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\phi}}}_{,{{r}}}}}} + {{{2}} {{{h_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\phi}}}}}}})}} & {{{r}^{2}}} {{({{{{cos\left(\theta\right)}} {{{h_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\phi}}}}}} + {{{sin\left(\theta\right)}} {{{h_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\phi}}}_{,{{\theta}}}}}}})}} & {{{h_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\phi}}}_{,{{\phi}}}}} {{{r}^{2}}} {{sin\left(\theta\right)}} \\ {{r}} {{{sin\left(\theta\right)}^{2}}} {{({{{{r}} {{{h_{\hat{\phi} \hat{\phi}}}_{,{{r}}}}}} + {{{2}} {{{h_{\hat{\phi} \hat{\phi}}}}}}})}} & {{{r}^{2}}} {{sin\left(\theta\right)}} {{({{{{sin\left(\theta\right)}} {{{h_{\hat{\phi} \hat{\phi}}}_{,{{\theta}}}}}} + {{{2}} {{cos\left(\theta\right)}} {{{h_{\hat{\phi} \hat{\phi}}}}}}})}} & {{{h_{\hat{\phi} \hat{\phi}}}_{,{{\phi}}}}} {{{r}^{2}}} {{{sin\left(\theta\right)}^{2}}} \end{matrix} \right] } \end{matrix} \right] }}$
${{\hat{D}_i}\left({{\epsilon}_j}_k\right)} = {{{{{{\epsilon}_j}_k}_{,i}} - {{{{{\epsilon}_j}_d}} {{{{{\hat{\Gamma}}^d}_i}_k}}}} - {{{{{\epsilon}_d}_k}} {{{{{\hat{\Gamma}}^d}_i}_j}}}}$
${{\hat{D}_i}\left({{\bar{\gamma}}_j}_k\right)} = {\overset{j\downarrow[{k\downarrow i\rightarrow}]}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} \left[ \begin{matrix} {h_{\hat{r} \hat{r}}}_{,{{r}}} & {{h_{\hat{r} \hat{r}}}_{,{{\theta}}}} - {{h_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\theta}}}}} + {{h_{\hat{r} \hat{r}}}}})}} & {{r}} {{({{{{h_{\hat{r} \hat{\theta}}}_{,{{\phi}}}} - {{{cos\left(\theta\right)}} {{{h_{\hat{r} \hat{\phi}}}}}}} - {{{sin\left(\theta\right)}} {{{h_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\phi}}}}}}})}} \\ {{{r}^{2}}} {{{h_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\theta}}}_{,{{r}}}}} & {{{r}^{2}}} {{({{{h_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\theta}}}_{,{{\theta}}}} + {{{2}} {{{h_{\hat{r} \hat{\theta}}}}}}})}} & {{{r}^{2}}} {{({{{h_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\theta}}}_{,{{\phi}}}} - {{{2}} {{cos\left(\theta\right)}} {{{h_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\phi}}}}}}})}} \\ {{{r}^{2}}} {{sin\left(\theta\right)}} {{{h_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\phi}}}_{,{{r}}}}} & {{{r}^{2}}} {{sin\left(\theta\right)}} {{({{{h_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\phi}}}_{,{{\theta}}}} + {{h_{\hat{r} \hat{\phi}}}}})}} & {{{r}^{2}}} {{sin\left(\theta\right)}} {{({{{{h_{\hat{\theta} \hat{\phi}}}_{,{{\phi}}}} - Covariant derivatives of phi and alpha
${{\bar{D}_i}\left(\alpha\right)} = {{\overset{i\downarrow}{ \left[ \begin{matrix} \alpha_{,{{r}}} \\ \alpha_{,{{\theta}}} \\ \alpha_{,{{\phi}}} \end{matrix} \right] }}_i}$
